93 #define EFM32_USB_CTRL_OFFSET 0x00000 /* System Control Register */
94 #define EFM32_USB_STATUS_OFFSET 0x00004 /* System Status Register */
95 #define EFM32_USB_IF_OFFSET 0x00008 /* Interrupt Flag Register */
96 #define EFM32_USB_IFS_OFFSET 0x0000c /* Interrupt Flag Set Register */
97 #define EFM32_USB_IFC_OFFSET 0x00010 /* Interrupt Flag Clear Register */

100 
101 #define EFM32_USB_GOTGCTL_OFFSET 0x3c000 /* OTG Control and Status Register */

112 #define EFM32_USB_DIEPTXF0_OFFSET 0x3c028 /* Endpoint 0 Transmit FIFO size */
113 #define EFM32_USB_GNPTXSTS_OFFSET 0x3c02c /* Non-periodic Transmit FIFO/Queue Status Register */

499 /* USB Register Bit Field Definitions ******************************************************************************************/
500 
501 /* Bit fields for USB CTRL */
502 
503 #define _USB_CTRL_RESETVALUE 0x00000000UL /* Default value for USB_CTRL */
504 #define _USB_CTRL_MASK 0x03330003UL /* Mask for USB_CTRL */
505 
506 #define USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP (0x1UL << 0) /* VBUSEN Active Polarity */
507 #define _USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP_SHIFT 0 /* Shift value for USB_VBUSENAP */
508 #define _USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP_MASK 0x1UL /* Bit mask for USB_VBUSENAP */
509 #define _USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP_DEFAULT 0x00000000UL /* Mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
510 #define _USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP_LOW 0x00000000UL /* Mode LOW for USB_CTRL */
511 #define _USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP_HIGH 0x00000001UL /* Mode HIGH for USB_CTRL */
512 #define USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP_DEFAULT (_USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP_DEFAULT << 0) /* Shifted mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
513 #define USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP_LOW (_USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP_LOW << 0) /* Shifted mode LOW for USB_CTRL */
514 #define USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP_HIGH (_USB_CTRL_VBUSENAP_HIGH << 0) /* Shifted mode HIGH for USB_CTRL */
515 #define USB_CTRL_DMPUAP (0x1UL << 1) /* DMPU Active Polarity */
516 #define _USB_CTRL_DMPUAP_SHIFT 1 /* Shift value for USB_DMPUAP */
517 #define _USB_CTRL_DMPUAP_MASK 0x2UL /* Bit mask for USB_DMPUAP */
518 #define _USB_CTRL_DMPUAP_DEFAULT 0x00000000UL /* Mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
519 #define _USB_CTRL_DMPUAP_LOW 0x00000000UL /* Mode LOW for USB_CTRL */
520 #define _USB_CTRL_DMPUAP_HIGH 0x00000001UL /* Mode HIGH for USB_CTRL */
521 #define USB_CTRL_DMPUAP_DEFAULT (_USB_CTRL_DMPUAP_DEFAULT << 1) /* Shifted mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
522 #define USB_CTRL_DMPUAP_LOW (_USB_CTRL_DMPUAP_LOW << 1) /* Shifted mode LOW for USB_CTRL */
523 #define USB_CTRL_DMPUAP_HIGH (_USB_CTRL_DMPUAP_HIGH << 1) /* Shifted mode HIGH for USB_CTRL */
524 #define USB_CTRL_VREGDIS (0x1UL << 16) /* Voltage Regulator Disable */
525 #define _USB_CTRL_VREGDIS_SHIFT 16 /* Shift value for USB_VREGDIS */
526 #define _USB_CTRL_VREGDIS_MASK 0x10000UL /* Bit mask for USB_VREGDIS */
527 #define _USB_CTRL_VREGDIS_DEFAULT 0x00000000UL /* Mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
528 #define USB_CTRL_VREGDIS_DEFAULT (_USB_CTRL_VREGDIS_DEFAULT << 16) /* Shifted mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
529 #define USB_CTRL_VREGOSEN (0x1UL << 17) /* VREGO Sense Enable */
530 #define _USB_CTRL_VREGOSEN_SHIFT 17 /* Shift value for USB_VREGOSEN */
531 #define _USB_CTRL_VREGOSEN_MASK 0x20000UL /* Bit mask for USB_VREGOSEN */
532 #define _USB_CTRL_VREGOSEN_DEFAULT 0x00000000UL /* Mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
533 #define USB_CTRL_VREGOSEN_DEFAULT (_USB_CTRL_VREGOSEN_DEFAULT << 17) /* Shifted mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
534 #define _USB_CTRL_BIASPROGEM01_SHIFT 20 /* Shift value for USB_BIASPROGEM01 */
535 #define _USB_CTRL_BIASPROGEM01_MASK 0x300000UL /* Bit mask for USB_BIASPROGEM01 */
536 #define _USB_CTRL_BIASPROGEM01_DEFAULT 0x00000000UL /* Mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
537 #define USB_CTRL_BIASPROGEM01_DEFAULT (_USB_CTRL_BIASPROGEM01_DEFAULT << 20) /* Shifted mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
538 #define _USB_CTRL_BIASPROGEM23_SHIFT 24 /* Shift value for USB_BIASPROGEM23 */
539 #define _USB_CTRL_BIASPROGEM23_MASK 0x3000000UL /* Bit mask for USB_BIASPROGEM23 */
540 #define _USB_CTRL_BIASPROGEM23_DEFAULT 0x00000000UL /* Mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
541 #define USB_CTRL_BIASPROGEM23_DEFAULT (_USB_CTRL_BIASPROGEM23_DEFAULT << 24) /* Shifted mode DEFAULT for USB_CTRL */
542 
543 /* Bit fields for USB STATUS */
544 
545 #define _USB_STATUS_RESETVALUE 0x00000000UL /* Default value for USB_STATUS */
546 #define _USB_STATUS_MASK 0x00000001UL /* Mask for USB_STATUS */
547 
548 #define USB_STATUS_VREGOS (0x1UL << 0) /* VREGO Sense Output */
549 #define _USB_STATUS_VREGOS_SHIFT 0 /* Shift value for USB_VREGOS */
550 #define _USB_STATUS_VREGOS_MASK 0x1UL /* Bit mask for USB_VREGOS */
551 #define _USB_STATUS_VREGOS_DEFAULT 0x00000000UL /* Mode DEFAULT for USB_STATUS */
552 #define USB_STATUS_VREGOS_DEFAULT (_USB_STATUS_VREGOS_DEFAULT << 0) /* Shifted mode DEFAULT for USB_STATUS */
553 
554 /* Bit fields for USB IF */
555 
556 #define _USB_IF_RESETVALUE 0x00000003UL /* Default value for USB_IF */
557 #define _USB_IF_MASK 0x00000003UL /* Mask for USB_IF */
558 
559 #define USB_IF_VREGOSH (0x1UL << 0) /* VREGO Sense High Interrupt Flag */
560 #define _USB_IF_VREGOSH_SHIFT 0 /* Shift value for USB_VREGOSH */
561 #define _USB_IF_VREGOSH_MASK 0x1UL /* Bit mask for USB_VREGOSH */
562 #define _USB_IF_VREGOSH_DEFAULT 0x00000001UL /* Mode DEFAULT for USB_IF */
563 #define USB_IF_VREGOSH_DEFAULT (_USB_IF_VREGOSH_DEFAULT << 0) /* Shifted mode DEFAULT for USB_IF */
564 #define USB_IF_VREGOSL (0x1UL << 1) /* VREGO Sense Low Interrupt Flag */
565 #define _USB_IF_VREGOSL_SHIFT 1 /* Shift value for USB_VREGOSL */
566 #define _USB_IF_VREGOSL_MASK 0x2UL /* Bit mask for USB_VREGOSL */
567 #define _USB_IF_VREGOSL_DEFAULT 0x00000001UL /* Mode DEFAULT for USB_IF */
568 #define USB_IF_VREGOSL_DEFAULT (_USB_IF_VREGOSL_DEFAULT << 1) /* Shifted mode DEFAULT for USB_IF */
569 
570 /* Bit fields for USB IFS */
571 
572 #define _USB_IFS_RESETVALUE 0x00000000UL /* Default value for USB_IFS */
573 #define _USB_IFS_MASK 0x00000003UL /* Mask for USB_IFS */
574 
575 #define USB_IFS_VREGOSH (0x1UL << 0) /* Set VREGO Sense High Interrupt Flag */
576 #define _USB_IFS_VREGOSH_SHIFT 0 /* Shift value for USB_VREGOSH */
577 #define _USB_IFS_VREGOSH_MASK 0x1UL /* Bit mask for USB_VREGOSH */
578 #define _USB_IFS_VREGOSH_DEFAULT 0x00000000UL /* Mode DEFAULT for USB_IFS */
579 #define USB_IFS_VREGOSH_DEFAULT (_USB_IFS_VREGOSH_DEFAULT << 0) /* Shifted mode DEFAULT for USB_IFS */
580 #define USB_IFS_VREGOSL (0x1UL << 1) /* Set VREGO Sense Low Interrupt Flag */
581 #define _USB_IFS_VREGOSL_SHIFT 1 /* Shift value for USB_VREGOSL */
582 #define _USB_IFS_VREGOSL_MASK 0x2UL /* Bit mask for USB_VREGOSL */
583 #define _USB_IFS_VREGOSL_DEFAULT 0x00000000UL /* Mode DEFAULT for USB_IFS */
584 #define USB_IFS_VREGOSL_DEFAULT (_USB_IFS_VREGOSL_DEFAULT << 1) /* Shifted mode DEFAULT for USB_IFS */
585 
586 /* Bit fields for USB IFC */
587
